It has come to my attention that several of you are asking for a little bit of flexibility on the School part with regards to the recent UTM Circular which states that Teaching & Learning activities including the final exam (F.E) will be conducted face to face and/or blended.

As we know, Dengue has become a global public health problem. Despite reactive efforts by the government in Malaysia, the dengue cases are on the increase although in pandemic. Hence, this study aims to assess the factors associated with dengue knowledge, attitude and practice (KAP) from public to find a way to prevent the increasing of dengue case.


Please help us by going through and fill in this survey:

Duration: 3 months (1st July - 30th Sept 2022)
Allowances: RM7/hour (up to RM1232/month)


Position Description: This position is intended for a student who is willing to work in a laboratory physically. It is based on an industrial project that focuses on technical aspects including (but not limited to):
1. 3D scanning 
2. 3D modeling/designing 
3. 3D printing 
4. Post-processing of the 3D printed 
5. Document preparation
The project is mainly focused on developing an Adaptive Assistive Device (AAD) for disabled persons. For example, prosthetic hand/leg, orthosis/braces, and other related rehabilitation devices. Working in the laboratory is a must since the candidate should utilize a 3D scanner and 3D printer.  


Skills Required: 
Only basic knowledge
1. CAD/CAE knowledge 
2. Biomechanics knowledge 
3. Biomaterial knowledge 
4. 3D printing knowledge 
5. Good communication skills 
6. Good presentation skills

05/10/2022, 7:31 am - Omar Fahmi | عُمَر: Assalamualaikum wbt and Good Day, 
 
Dear Students, 
 
The following news dated 1st October 2022 on the recent UTM restructuring exercises are referred : 
 
Kenyataan rasmi utm melaksanakan penstrukturan semula entiti akademik untuk kelestarian bidang tujahan university 
 
In summary, our previous entity, the School of Biomedical Engineering and Health Sciences (SBEHS) is now a part of the Faculty of Electrical Engineering (FEE) and known as the Department of Biomedical Engineering and Health Sciences (DBEHS) effective 1st October 2022.  
 
In terms of the academic-related matters for both UG and PG, there will be no changes as of now, teaching and learning activities including lectures, tutorials and labs will be held in our satellite building (V01). 
 
The following are the coordinators and person-in-charge for academic-related in the Department of Biomedical Engineering and Health Sciences : 
 
Undergraduate Coordinator (Biomedical Engineering) : Dr. Hau Yuan Wen (hauyuanwen@utm.my) 
Undergraduate Coordinator (Equine Management) : Dr. Fuziaton Baharudin (fuziaton@utm.my) 
Final Year Undergraduate Project 1 Coordinator (Biomedical Engineering) : Dr. Mohamad Ikhwan Jamaludin (mohamad.ikhwan@utm.my) 
Final Year Undergraduate Project 2 Coordinator  (Biomedical Engineering) : Dr. Raimi Dewan @ Abdul Rahman (raimi.dar@utm.my) 
Final Year Undergraduate Project 1 & 2 Coordinator (Equine Management) : Dr. Mira Panadi (mirapanadi@utm.my)  
Postgraduate Coordinator (Taught Course ) : Dr. Siti Ruzita Mahmod (sruzita@utm.my) 
Postgraduate Coordinator (Research) : Dr. Izwyn Zulkapri (izwyn@utm.my) 
Undergraduate Academic Office : Madam Zulbaidah Muhammad (ugskbsk@biomedical.utm.my) 
Postgraduate Academic Office : Madam Noor Hafizah Rahamad (pgskbsk@biomedical.utm.my) 
 
If there is any further inquiry regarding academic-related matters please do not hesitate to contact them.  
 
We wish you all the best in the upcoming session (2022/2023) and would like to welcome you to the Department of Biomedical Engineering and Health Sciences, Faculty of Electrical Engineering!  
 
-- 
Best Regards,

10/10/2022, 11:07 am - Omar Fahmi | عُمَر: Assalamualaikum wbt  and Good Day


To all Lecturers and Students (Department of Biomedical Engineering and Health Sciences),


As all of you are aware, the first week of 2022/2023 semester 1 will start on 16th October 2022, which is coincidentally the last week for some of the upcoming fourth (4th) year students undergoing their official industrial training. 


There are some concerns as brought out by the MPP representatives and a few other queries from the students, that there will be instances students could not attend the physical class session in the first week. We have brought this issue to the new FKE Academic Committee and following the internal discussion, it has been decided that all classes will resume face-to-face including service subjects from other FKE departments. 


However, for the affected 4th-year students, kindly inform your respective lecturer regarding your situation and depending on the lecturers' plan for their T&L activities,  they may be able to conduct the class online to accommodate you.  


See you all soon!


Many thanks 


--
Best Regards,

Dear ALL FINAL SEMESTER Students, 
 
APPLICATION FOR CONFERMENT OF DEGREE (GRADUATION) FOR SEMESTER I SESSION 2022/2023 
 
For all students who are in FINAL SEMESTER and will graduate this Semester I Session 2022/2023, please fill up the form as attached for your Conferment of Degree (Graduation).  
 
The form must be signed by your AA and attached with your IC (local students) / passport copy (international students) and submit all the documents before or on 6 JANUARY 2023. 
 
Please MAKE SURE you are fulfilling all the requirements for the conferment degree : 
> Attain a total of NOT LESS than 137 credit hours with a minimum CGPA of 2.0 
> COMPLETED all the Professional Skill Certificate (PSC) Courses - THREE COMPULSORY courses and TWO ELECTIVES courses.


The documents can be email to ugskbsk@biomedical.utm.my
 
Thank you,

ارجوا أن تكونوا في أتم صحة وعافية


بعد الفصل الدراسي هذا سيكون موعد التدريب العملي ( Internship ) لدفعتي وأرجوا منكم مساعدتي قليلًا.


للطلبة الذين تدربوا هنا في ماليزيا، هل يمكنكم كتابة اسم الشركة او المستشفى التي تدربتم بها مع وصف مختصر لتجربتكم ونصائحكم، وطرق للتواصل مع الشركة كذلك لتسهيل عملية التواصل معهم وتأمين فرصة لديهم.


علما أنني سأقوم بجمع المعلومات هذه لمشاركتها مع طلبة كثر، عرب وغير عرب للفائدة، ولكم جزيل الشكر .

21/01/2025, 9:20 am - +60 11-3984 4367: السلام عليكم جميعا, 


تحتاج الأمانة الأكاديمية إلى مساعدتكم العاجلة. نرجو منكم مشاركة أي موارد متاحة لدعم مجتمعنا وتعزيزه. نقدّر مساهمتكم بشدة، ونتطلع إلى دعمكم. 
 
المساعدة فيها خير كبير لكم كما قال الله تعالى: "يرفع الله الذين آمنوا منكم والذين أوتوا العلم درجات" (سورة المجادلة: 11)


و عن عبد الله بن عمر رضي الله عنهما قال: قال رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم: "أحب الناس إلى الله أنفعهم للناس، وأحب الأعمال إلى الله عز وجل سرور تدخله على مسلم، أو تكشف عنه كربة، أو تقضي عنه دينا، أو تطرد عنه جوعا" (رواه الطبراني في المعجم الكبير).


الرابط:
